resource\n\tevents := p.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\tp.logger.Info(\"Stopping PolicyQuotaController\")\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-events:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tp.logger.Info(\"Event channel closed\")\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif event.Kind == resource.Sync {\n\t\t\t\tp.logger.Debug(\"Received sync event, controller is synchronized\")\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tpolicy := event.Object\n\t\t\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\t// Check quota before allowing the policy\n\t\t\t\tif err := p.CheckQuota(namespace); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tp.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace: namespace,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tlogfields.K8sObjName:   policy.GetName(),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\"policy_count\":         p.getPolicyCount(namespace),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\"max_per_namespace\":    p.maxPerNamespace,\n\t\t\t\t\t}).Warn(\"Policy quota exceeded\")\n\t\t\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tp.incrementPolicyCount(namespace)\n\t\t\t\tp.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\t\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace: namespace,\n\t\t\t\t\tlogfields.K8sObjName:   policy.GetName(),\n\t\t\t\t\t\"policy_count\":         p.getPolicyCount(namespace),\n\t\t\t\t}).Debug(\"Policy added\")\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\tp.decrementPolicyCount(namespace)\n\t\t\t\tp.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\t\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace: namespace,\n\t\t\t\t\tlogfields.K8sObjName:   policy.GetName(),\n\t\t\t\t\t\"policy_count\":         p.getPolicyCount(namespace),\n\t\t\t\t}).Debug(\"Policy deleted\")\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// CheckQuota checks if a policy can be created in the given namespace.\n// It returns an error if the namespace quota has been exceeded.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tp.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer p.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tcurrentCount := p.policyCounts[namespace]\n\tif currentCount >= p.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%w: namespace=%s, current=%d, max=%d\",\n\t\t\tErrQuotaExceeded, namespace, currentCount, p.maxPerNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// incrementPolicyCount increments the policy count for a namespace.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) incrementPolicyCount(namespace string) {\n\tp.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer p.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tp.policyCounts[namespace]++\n}\n\n// decrementPolicyCount decrements the policy count for a namespace.\n// It does not allow the count to go below 0.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) decrementPolicyCount(namespace string) {\n\tp.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer p.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tif p.policyCounts[namespace] > 0 {\n\t\tp.policyCounts[namespace]--\n\t}\n}\n\n// getPolicyCount returns the current policy count for a namespace.\n// This is a helper method that requires the lock to already be held.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) getPolicyCount(namespace string) int {\n\tp.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer p.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\treturn p.policyCounts[namespace]\n}\n\n// GetNamespacePolicyCounts returns a copy of the current policy counts per namespace.\n// This method is primarily useful for testing and monitoring.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) GetNamespacePolicyCounts() map[string]int {\n\tp.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer p.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tcounts := make(map[string]int)\n\tfor ns, count := range p.policyCounts {\n\t\tcounts[ns] = count\n\t}\n\n\treturn counts\n}\n"}}
